Here is the situation:\\ \tt \\ \tt WHAT: Things at places\\ \tt LEFT: fork\\ \tt RIGHT: pencils\\ \tt TOP: screwdriver\\ \tt BOTTOM: screws\\ \tt CENTER: blouse\\ \tt NORTHWEST: accordion\\ \tt NORTHEAST: frying pan\\ \tt SOUTHWEST: blush\\ \tt SOUTHEAST: bikini\\ \tt HERE: watermelon\\ \tt THERE: nails\\ \tt NOWHERE: buttercup\\ \tt EVERYWHERE: ladder\\ \tt INSIDE: pansy\\ \tt OUTSIDE: teaspoon\\ \tt \\ \tt Questions from the questioner will start with QUESTIONER. Please reply in the form: ANSWER: <one sentence>\\ \tt \\ \tt I will also ask you questions. These questions will start with ME: . Please answer these questions with: ASIDE: <one sentence>\\ \tt \\ \tt Important: Give short, direct answers!\\ \tt \\ \tt Let us start. 
	  }

	   }

    & & & \multicolumn{2}{p{0.3\linewidth}}{\cellcolor[rgb]{0.95,0.95,0.95}{%
	\makecell[{{p{\linewidth}}}]{% 
	  \tt {\tiny [GM$|$GM]}  
	 Answer is correct. 
	  } 
	   } 
	   } 
	 & & \\ 
 

    \theutterance \stepcounter{utterance}  

    & & & \multicolumn{2}{p{0.3\linewidth}}{\cellcolor[rgb]{0.95,0.95,0.95}{%
	\makecell[{{p{\linewidth}}}]{% 
	  \tt {\tiny [GM$|$GM]}  
	 End probing 
	  } 
	   } 
	   } 
	 & & \\ 
 

    \theutterance \stepcounter{utterance}  

    & & & \multicolumn{2}{p{0.3\linewidth}}{\cellcolor[rgb]{0.95,0.95,0.95}{%
	\makecell[{{p{\linewidth}}}]{% 
	  \tt {\tiny [GM$|$GM]}  
	 Game finished. 
	  }

	 & & \\ 
 

\end{supertabular}
